## Limitation for Move count/Draft/TS Cap

受信: Thu Jul 03 2025 15:24:38 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Ko Murakami \<ko.murakami@one-line.com\>  
\*AX1:Move count Limitation for CLIQQ\*

・AX1のCLIQQ向けでは揚げ地Move countの制限あり、250unitがMaxload。

→これを超えないために(50/75/50/25/50 per KR/JP/CPRC+NPRC/XMN/OTHERS)という積地側での制限も設けている。

→このため、稀にAPあるにも関わらずBKGがリリースされずに引き受け可否に関して問い合わせが入るが、基本的に250unit

に達していないので、リリース可能と伝える。(IQQ MovecountはLookerで定期的に配信される)

→Latin America側輸入250 Units、LA輸出XXXUnitsと決めらているが、これを大きく上回る場合は、現地側へ連絡。（超過した分、

LA輸出側が通常よりも積載できなくなるため）

→このMove countは昔に決められた模様。ターミナルのProductivityに起因。

→各港のBerth Windowに拠るもので、停泊可能時間に対して何Unit荷役（＝ターミナルのProductivity）できるか。

→例として8時間停泊できる場合、1時間あたり100unitのProductivityであれば、800unitが丸船での最大荷役数量であり、これを各

OperatorのBSAで按分し、その後輸出入で分割。

→特段特性のある輸出港/輸入港でなければ、マッチバックが基本なので50：50が輸出入の基本ではある。

\*AX2:Allocation for CSE cargo\*

・AX2ではCSE(Caribbean Sea)向けの貨物のALCが150TEU程度ある。

→EC1がPAMITへ寄港しなくなったため、AX-2のPAROD経由でAL5(Trans Atranticのサービスで、北米西岸-カリブ海-北欧州)

を使用し、DOCAU(DP world Caucedo@Dominican Republic)へ輸送。

\*AX2:Draft Limitation at COBUN\*

・AX2ではCOBUNでのDraft Limitationがある。

→Non ONE vesselsであれば問題ないが、ONE vesselsのとき(＝大型船＝通常よりも我々のBSAが大きい)は注視。

＞Small vessel 28,327MT

＞Big vessel 35,827MT

\*AX3:Draft Limitation at GTPRQ\*

・AX3航路はGTPRQ(PUERTO QQUETZAL＠GUATEMARA)でのDraft Limitation(17,000MT at 11.8m)

がある。

・AX3はMX-GT-CO-PEの寄港順でMXZLO/MXZLC/PECLLがAX1-AX3とで重複する港だが、GT寄港時に上記制限を下回る必要がある。

→GT前のMX(ESE/ZLO)の貨物シフトは意味がない。AX-1に貨物をシフトする場合はGT以降で且つAX1と重複するPECLL向けの貨物をシフト。

\*AX4:Minimum Target for MXZLO\*

・ 必達数量は \*500-600TEUs \*(当初ZLO寄港がなかった為、AdhocCall扱いにて500TEUを超えないと寄港のメリットがない)

・T/S at MXZLO is NOT accepted （MXZLO寄港はT/Sしないオペレーションのため、ZLO CYもしくはMX Doorのみ）

\*AX4:Transshipment CAP at MXZLC\*

・トランシップ可能な数量は \*500Unit\* (T/Sは500UNITまで。LZC CYもしくはMX Doorはカウントされない)

・Priority of T/S, only MAR and MX2 services can connect via MXZLC.

1\)    For SVAQJ, which can only be transported via MX2

2\)    For GTPRQ, which can only be transported via MAR

3\)    For NICIO \+ CRCAL, which is served by MAR, is currently being

transported via COBUN on the MX3 route.)

もしAX4 のスペースに余裕があり、MX3 がすでに満載であれば、この選択肢（AX4経由MARでのNICIOやCRCAL向けの輸送を検討）

\--

peak season will start soon and market volume will increase in coming

weeks, particularly the 2nd half of July.

situation.

I will extend the existing NOR rate until 21 July 2025 for now.

According to the Virtual Office Guideline

\<https://drive.google.com/file/d/1kZ17CMKedQTpKzAIi4GNIC8lai7hgi4k/view?usp=sharing\>

and with the EA’s Goal-Setting timeline, here are some notes for the

appraisers to ensure a smooth process

\*Alignment and Agreement\*

   \- Both home and host country appraisers should \*align, discuss, and

   agree\* on the employee's performance comments during all phases of the

   appraisal process.

   \- ONE has a standardized approach to evaluating KARs, KPIs, and Core

   Values \*to ensure greater consistency and clarity\* across all

   evaluations.

   \- Definition guidelines are \*embedded in the SF forms\* throughout the

   year for better alignment.

   \- In the Core Value section, \*all eight core values must be inputted\*.

   If the appraisee did not input the corresponding comment, please reject and

   send the form back to the appraisee for adjustment.

   \- KAR/KPI/CV weighting distribution: KARs (30%), KPIs(30%), and Core

   Values (40%)

\*EA Timeline\*

\*Description\*

\*Target Deadline\*

KAR/KPI/Core Value setting.

## Jun-Sep PL Projection (Deadline 27th May '25)

受信: Fri May 16 2025 12:01:42 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Elvie Loke \<elvie.loke@one-line.com\>  
Hi All,

Firstly, let us share with you on the changes in the PL forecast cycle

effective from Jun. Unlike previous years, we will not be required to

prepare 2HBP. Instead, we will need to prepare a 7 months forecast which

will follow the usual forecast practice rather than the budget process. No

change to the full year budget which timeline to be shared in due course.

Pls refer to the new forecast cycle below for your reference:

\[image: image.png\]

This time, we need to review and prepare a 4 month forecast for Jun-Sep

period. Pls find the working sheet in the link below.

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1TyTfAbG-SFAFv0j90UPl1D-z2C-zFHVgvIGCj\_dsViI/edit?usp=drive\_link

Deadline for submission: \* 27th May (Tue) COB your time\*

   \- As usual, please \*review and update BSA, Utilization, Lifting, FRT,

   L/M/S ratio, GRI, CM & FAK rate\*.

   \- Please input comments for significant changes under the worksheet

   named “\*Key Notes\*”.

   \- Pls make sure to update \*Actual Result/Latest Projection for\* \*Week

   21 \* (last week of May '25)

   \- Pls make sure to update ALL figures directly into Google Sheet Link

   provided above. \*Pls do not send separate excel files.\*

   \- Lastly, \*pls ensure to work on “pink” cells only and\* \*DO NOT\* \*overwrite

   the formula cells with values or change the formula.\*

Pls let us know if you need any assistance or clarification. Thanks\!

□---------------------------------□

Elvie Loke

Marketing & Commercial

Africa and Latin America Trade

□---------------------------------□

Ocean Network Express Pte. Ltd.

7 Straits View

\#16-01 Marina One East Tower

\*To all GHQ SYM/DYM Leaders\*

We're starting to plan for DDE Program Increment 17 (PI17), covering June

2025 to Aug 2025\. To ensure your reporting needs are considered, please

submit any requests for new Looker Explore/Dashboard requests \*by May 27th\*.

Please submit your requests to \[GHQ M\&C Data CoE (

ghq.mc.data.coe@one-line.com)\] with the following information:

   \- \*BI Request Summary:\* A brief description of the explore/dashboard.

   \- \*Business Justification/Business Use Case:\* Explain why this is needed

   and how it will be used.

   \- \*Data Points/Source:\* Identify the data required and where it's

   located if possible.

\*Important Notes:\*

   \- \*Scope: \*This is for new explore/dashboard demand, please raise RSD in

   case of enhancement request for the existing Looker explore as usual manner.

   \- \*Prioritization:\* All requests will be reviewed alongside regional

   demands and prioritized based on business needs and available capacity.

   \- \*Development Timeline:\* While development will begin in PI17,

   completion within the same PI cannot be guaranteed.

   \- \*Next Steps:\* If your request is approved for PI17, Data CoE Portfolio

   Manager/KPI Ambassador will contact you in February to prepare detailed

   business specifications and SR.

Thank you for your understanding.

GHQ M\&C Data CoE

## TT Tool Data Quality Enhancement

受信: Tue May 13 2025 08:00:00 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kenichi Michida \<kenichi.michida@one-line.com\>  
\*仲井さん、\*

おはようございます。

すでに、KKEから何らかのアプローチがあったかもしれませんが、先日KKEオフィスを訪問した際に、TT

Toolに関する分析内容をご照会頂きましたので、シェアさせて頂きます。

添付のPPT資料のP3-P7（就中、P5及びP6がその根幹だと思いますが）について記載があります。また、別途元ネタのエクセルのリンクをご展開申し上げます（データ分量が多すぎてアクセスしにくいですが）。

これらをベースに、それぞれのデータの問題点をきちんと認識して、対応策を取っていってもらえると助かります。必要であれば、PRD

Teamへも展開しますので、仰って下さい。

また、KKEさんを招請したセッションを設定したほうが良ければ、仰ってくださいませ。

\*（分析内容）\*

\*差異分析（前回比較）\*

Ocean Priorityについては、Lower

PriorityのRouteを包含するかどうかで、結果が変わってくると思われます。あとは、Inland

Masterの設定問題が足を引っ張っているので、ここに対応策（事前に問題になるLocationやVendorを特定してクリーンアップする）を検討できれば、状況はもう少し安定するかと思います。

\[image: image.png\]

\*PS Dataとの差異分析\*

\[image: image.png\]

これは、当方の理解ですが、以下のとおりです。まず以て、このCover率は流石に低すぎるので、基本は90％以上を目指す等の明確な指針が必要だと思います。そのうえで、各ポイントに付いてプロセスで対応を検討する必要があるかと。

①、No enough priority PRD Ocean data（30.2％）

：単純にPriorityに制限を掛けている点が問題点なので、外すことで対応かのうかと。

②、No SLAN in Manual Proforma（18.1％）：これはAd-hocのTT Tool作成時に必要なService

Laneが定義されていない（Proformaとして）だけなので、これもデータの問題かと思います。

③、No POR\_CD in Inland Master（16.7％）：こちらはInland Location

Codeの漏れだとおもうので、なるべくTender DBのデータを活用してVariationを増やすような算段が必要かと思います。

④、No PRD Ocean Route（11.9％）：こちらはOcean

Routeがないということなので、そもそも当該サービスがない可能性もあり、対応が難しいかもしれません。

⑤、No valid Service Proforma（8.0％）：こちらも対応策は別途検討が必要かも。単純に設定が抜けていただけなのかが不明です。

⑥、No Outbound location pair in Inland Master（4.3％）：これもInland

Masterの設定（VendorとRoute Patternの不一致も含むのかもしれませんが）に起因するものなので、対応策はあるはずかと。

/////quote/////

元ネタデータ

\*\[3\] TT Tool の Missing Routeの分析データについて\*

\*\[3.1\] PS data に対するMissing route\*

PS dataに対するMissing routeとその原因について、以下のファイルにまとめています。

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/17XkPOn4K4HkKAvQYpukf2xJY7SlrUwea/edit?usp=drive\_link\&ouid=104322637348619358203\&rtpof=true\&sd=true

・2025/4/4に実行依頼のあったデータと「27 Mar 2025」のPS dataを比較した結果です。

・Summaryのシートで、各原因と件数をまとめています。

・Sampleのシートで、具体的なデータを使って各原因のもとになっているテーブル等の説明をしています。

・1 Routeごとの詳細なMissingの原因については、Service Scope Group名のシートに出力しています。

\*\[3.2\] 前回との比較\*

前回実行時からのなくなっているRoute、追加されているRouteのについて

Tradeごとにまとめたファイルを、以下の場所まとめています。

https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/14IKRCLw6pxP9FAgHfmCiofzG1yiwAJFX?usp=drive\_link

///unquote/////

## Eagle X members' Task Management

受信: Mon May 05 2025 08:00:00 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Koji Nakai \<koji.nakai@one-line.com\>  
Hi Team,

(cc Eagle X management)

Hope you are doing well.

While I understand that this request may feel a bit cumbersome, I would

sincerely appreciate your cooperation from the standpoint of managing a

large team like Eagle X.

In the past, we implemented a similar approach within SYM Eagle X, and the

primary objective remains unchanged: to gain visibility into the weekly

tasks being handled by team members at the Assistant Manager level and

below.

Given the highly flexible nature of our work environment including work from

 home and virtual office, it is important for both myself and the Managers

to have a clear understanding of each team member’s ongoing

responsibilities.

Just as you observe and assess the performance of your direct managers, it

is equally essential for Assistant Manager to consistently perform at a

level above that of Senior Executive and Executive.

Likewise, Senior Executive are expected to deliver results exceeding those

of Executive.

While my overall management style emphasizes autonomy and self-direction, I

believe that a certain degree of performance oversight is necessary to

ensure team effectiveness.

To that end, we kindly ask that you input your weekly tasks for the three

upcoming off-peak months (May through July). Please see \*Task Management\*

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1egAVf\_rnDrpI3LZ-ahbkpZEFjvwMbt8BAq7WgKJeC38/edit?gid=685156715\#gid=685156715\>

.

Please include completed tasks as well as those still in progress. For any

pending items, I would appreciate it if you could also indicate your

anticipated completion timeline.

Thank you very much for your understanding. Should you have any questions

or concerns, please feel free to reach out.

Best regards,

Koji Nakai

Digital Yield Management

Contract Management Team

Eagle X Unit

## Re: Pre-conversion for ASIS accounts in FY25 live

受信: Thu Mar 27 2025 10:26:23 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kiwi Ngai \<kiwi.ngai@one-line.com\>  
Hi Masuda-san,

Regarding the JBG tender, I'd like to provide some additional information.

The JBG tender was initially a trial to explore a joint tender approach for

Unilever, Electrolux, and Mondelez. However, after the first round,

Electrolux decided to withdraw and has confirmed they will not participate

in a joint tender next year.

Therefore, for the pre-conversion process:

\* \*\*Electrolux:\*\* to use the Round 2 file for pre-conversion as suggested

by Mariel.

\* \*\*Unilever:\*\* Since the JBG Round 2 file combines the volumes for both

Unilever and Mondelez, and we are unsure if they will take the same

approach next tender season, I recommend holding off on pre-conversion for

Unilever at this time. If this is a must to do a preconversion, a note need

to be remarks to inform the audience it involve 2 tender's data

Best Regards,

      conversion process.

   the file is overly complicated, please let us know so we can consider how

   to handle them on a case-by-case basis.

## Dashboard Request Completed \- "Result (Pricing)" Storypoint

受信: Tue Mar 18 2025 16:28:00 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daniel Woo \<daniel.woo@one-line.com\>  
Hi Masuda-san,

This dashboard request which you had asked for last week has been

completed. It will tell us \*how on-time each trade's pricers submissions\*

are.

Let me know if there is any question. Also, if there is no feedback, I will

roll this out by tomorrow afternoon.

\*Result (Pricing) \- On-Time (%)\*

   \- Request means that for the specific account/sequence/round (or a/s/r),

   that trade needs to submit the pricing.

   \- On-Time means that the submission date of the trade is before or on

   the day of Pricing Deadline.

   \- Late / Omit means that either the submission is done after the Pricing

   Deadline or there is no submission at all.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Result (Pricing) \- On-Time (%)\*

   \- This will give an indication on which trade (2-digit) is most timely,

   and which is the least timely.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Result (Pricing) \- On-Time (%) \[Top 20 / Bottom 20\]\*

   \- This allows the managements to deep dive into which of the specific

   trades are on-time and which are not on-time.

   \- As we can see, TA\_NonDomi-SCM is the least timely, while LW\_NonDomi-SC

   is the most timely. Sometimes, this value can be skewed due to small

   numbers (some only had \<10 requests)

\[image: image.png\]

\*Pricing Request to Pricing Deadline (per Round)\*

   \- This provides information on the median number of days we are giving

   pricers to quote. The higher the better.

\[image: image.png\]

Thanks and Regards,

Daniel Woo

Flourance and Leandro, and supported by the rest of the Eagle-X members (for

Masuda-san to arrange). At the start of the month, Sori will need to pull

the previous month's LIVE data from the Conversion Tool. After that, the

Review Team will review all mappings with the status "Please Review

(Approve / Reject)". After that is completed, Sano-san is notified and will

upload the approved mappings into the OPUS Master Table.

The current average Place & Trade Mapping scores of CST, OMMC, and WNS

India are 4.61, 3.88 and 3.80 respectively. To rebuild the trust with North

America (especially for offshore tenders), we should aim to improve OMMC

and WNS India Place & Trade Mapping quality score to around 4.60 (which is

CST current average score for Place & Trade Mapping). Ideally, this

automation will indirectly benefit CST and raise their baseline score. (for

Masuda-san's reference)

In short, here are the key takeaways and my comments:

   \- Ryan has reviewed and approved the "Data Review" process.

   data is auto-mapped by the Master Table (this means the certainty of

   \- For Place Mapping, Nakai-san is handling it (ops team should handle

   this, rather than the product owner himself).

   \- Even though Consolidation data is ideal, for now we can use Conversion

   Tool data and manually review them for immediate benefits (as such, I

   believe the decision is to go with Conversion Tool data, which allows us to

   move fast and reap results fast).

Thanks and Regards,

Daniel Woo

In short, this email will mark the official start of the Data Review

Routine Process for \*Place Mapping\* and \*Trade Mapping\* respectively.

Please refer to the Data Review

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/190C83hemRWVh1KtYZOabZqMFlFJpAsPeATTVEuEVcho/edit?gid=2060478820\#gid=2060478820\>

Sheet for more information:

Tentatively, this process will be performed on a \*monthly \*basis, to

enhance our master tables as much as possible. To do that, we need to

review place mapping and trade mapping, to decide which are the ones to

include into the master table. This is important, because ultimately if our

master tables are comprehensive, the LIVE conversion process will be a much

more error-free process with faster turnaround.

For the April 2025 cycle, please refer to the following list for the

assigned reviewers.

this is the first review cycle we are doing), we hope this is

completed by \*14/April/2025

(Mon)\*.

Data Review process, so that it gets easier as time goes on. Feel free to

also let me know if there are suggestions to enhance this system as a

## Re: Approval Required: Need "③-1\_Place" Reference Sheet for "Place & Trade Mapping" Master Table

受信: Wed Apr 16 2025 15:44:23 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daniel Woo \<daniel.woo@one-line.com\>  
Hi all,

Thank you everyone for the inputs into the Data Review Sheet as well as

some enhancement suggestions. Here are some of the improvements done to the

Data Review sheet to improve overall efficiency:

\*A New Column to input the Correct ONE Code (applicable for those that are

marked as "Reject" initially)\*

   \- Previously, if you see the Place Mapping is incorrect, all you need to

   do is to mark it as either "Accept" or "Reject".

   \- Now, there is an additional step that you have to do. If you mark as

   "Reject", kindly put the correct ONE Code under Col. R.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Split "Skip (in Master Table)" into "Skip (in Master Table, Port Pair)"

and "Skip (in Master Table, Country Pair)"\*

   \- Basically, the previous logic did not take into account the matching

   Country Pair. Now, it is taking care of this part.

   \- On top of knowing the data is in the Master Table, it will tell us how

   it is auto mapped (either by Port Pair, or Country Pair).

   \- If both Port Pair and Country Pair are present, it will reflect as

   "Skip (in Master Table, Port Pair)", since that has a higher priority than

   the Country Pair match.

\[image: image.png\]

As of now, this is the status of the review progress. Please continue to

perform the review, thank you.

\[image: image.png\]

Hi Maha ( @S MAHALAKSHMI \<mahalakshmi.s@one-line.com\> ),

\*"Have covered Trade mapping upto extend, Rest we have no data found in the

opus for some of the Latin America Ports, Inland Ports etc."\*

For the comment you had above, correct me if I am wrong, you mentioned

there are a few mappings that have no data found in OPUS and it is also not

possible to apply the Country Pair logic. I want to know as of now, how is

the Conversion Team and the Eagle-X Team determining the service scope for

these cases?

From what I see, since there are only 17 rows of data that fall into this

category (as seen from the "Please Review (Approve / Reject)" under you),

it will not be important and urgent at this point (and we can just leave it

as what it is). But, if the logic is quite straight forward, you can DM me

so I can gather the requirements. Or else, you can also join our next

biweekly meeting at 29/April (Tues) 1PM to share more on this.

Thanks and Regards,

Daniel Woo

## グローバル医療保険導入のお知らせ

受信: Thu Feb 27 2025 13:00:00 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Atsuko Nakamura \<atsuko.nakamura@one-line.com\>  
各位、

このたび従来の海外旅行傷害保険及び医療費補助（既往症、歯科治療）から新たにCigna社のグローバル医療保険を導入することとなりました。

本保険は、海外駐在中の病気や怪我に対し、迅速かつ充実した医療サービスを提供するものです。

【導入開始日】  2025年4月1日

【概要及び導入背景】

\- グローバル医療保険：海外赴任者向け医療保険

‐ Cigna社：アメリカに本社を置く大手保険会社

‐ 従来の海外旅行傷害保険では適用されなかった既往症、歯科治療、人間ドック、予防接種、出産ケア及び家族計画もカバー

‐ 医療保険の充実化と会社への医療費精算プロセスを無くすことにより、社員及びご家族のプライバシーを守る

【対象者】 社員及び帯同している扶養家族（Work Pass (EP/SPass) 保持者・就労しているご家族は除く）。

ご家族が帰国・就労される際は、\<ghq.hr.im@one-line.com\>までにご連絡ください。

【保険料】

扶養家族を含む保険料の10％のコストをご負担いただくこととなります。（長期海外駐在を前提とした雇用形態のため、皆様にはより充実した保険内容を適応させていただきます。社員の皆様にも一部保険料をご負担いただくことで医療保険制度を安定的に維持できます。）

ご負担いただく保険料につきましては毎月の給与から天引きさせていただきます。また、保険料は毎年4月に見直しを行います。

【海外旅行傷害保険】 Cignaの導入にあたり、海外旅行傷害保険は2025年3月31日で廃止とさせていただきます。

3月までに発生したClaimは5月15日までに申請をお願い致します。

【健康保険】変更無し。引き続きご使用いただけます。

【入会手続き】3月中旬にCignaよりWelcome

e-mailが送付されますので、届きましたら添付資料をご確認の上アカウントのご登録をお願い致します。

入会手続きについてご不明点・ご質問がございましたら下記ブリーフィングセッション時にてCignaへご確認お願い致します。

3月下旬にCignaよりブリーフィングセッション（保険内容、入会手続き、申請方法等）を実施致します。

後日、Invitationをお送りさせていただきますので是非ご参加ください。

セッションの録画及び資料もご共有致しますので、ご都合が合わない場合はそちらをご覧ください。

宜しくお願い致します。

Atsuko Nakamura (中村敦子) \- ONE DEJIMA- GHR Mobility

Master.

(2) Requests Sano-san to extract the Consolidation Data based on our

handled Live Tenders as per my proposal during the meeting, however, this

is not possible as we do not have Consolidation Data in the Big Query as

per him.

(3) In view of that, I requested to have the ONE FORMAT data instead for

all customers and all rounds that we have processed already.

(4) Sano-san is able to provide this data which is around 300,000+ lanes.

(5) At the same time, requested CST to have their Trade Master Data for

comparison and they able to provide it the next week after.

Attached links are the files I have worked on the past weeks.

\*TRADE MAPPING Master as of 04/02/2024:\*

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1MbGm9mqCMNC0NAQNOIGG\_vnKpx98oCgT43eluPbPx-Y/edit?gid=681609980\#gid=681609980

\*CST Trade Mapping Data:\*

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/12V66d6f7yv6dRbwB6vcR6uNSYccSb-7YBJgz7\_WsYro/edit?pli=1\&gid=1336122218\#gid=1336122218

Based on initial observation, the data from \*CST Trade Mapping Data\* was

being used by CST is also based on the LIVE Tenders that we've handled

before consists of the below headers:

\[image: image.png\]

\*Total Portpairs: 61,587\*

While our current \*TRADE MAPPING Master\* consists of the following headers:

\[image: image.png\]

\*Total Portpairs: 101,308 Port to Port basis / 16,634 (Country to Country

basis)\*

On the other hand, the data that I have requested from Sano-san which is

based on the consolidated \*ONE Format \*from \*Big Query\* consists of the

following headers.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Total Portpairs: 300,730 (Including all LIVE Customers / All rounds)\*

With this huge number of lanes, I prefer to focus on the data coming from

the Big Query which I updated some of the blank service scopes manually by

using the SVC Scope API Tool and OPUS.

\*For the Comparison of the Data here's the result below:\*

\*CST Trade Mapping Data vs. ONE Format Big Query Data\*

(1) 61,200 out of 61,587 were already aligned with our ONE Format

consolidated data from the Big Query.

(2) 369 out of 61,587 are the portpairs that didn't match with each file

which needed further double checking.

(3) 18 out of 61,587 have no matching results from the ONE Format Bigquery

which needed further double checking.

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1gpIa6t1AtMrSu1prWe0ermPv5Or0dGPG7nkCY562C6U/edit?gid=0\#gid=0

\*Trade Mapping Master (Current) vs. ONE Format Big Query Data\*

(1) 27,369 out of 117,942 were already aligned with our ONE Format

consolidated data from the Big Query.

(2) 131 out 117,942 are the portpairs that didn't match with each file

which needed further double checking.

(3) 90,442 out of 117,942 have no matching results from the ONE Format Big

Query hence these lanes will be part of the new consolidated Trade Mapping

Master Data along with the ONE Format Big Query data as the main Trade

Mapping Master source.

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1zAJ6RfIGZFNA5Tg-0hJaRrZblduWQ71l59rjhKQKxZI/edit?gid=2048854189\#gid=2048854189

Dear Benhur,

Thanks for your email.

Please find our comments below with yellow highlighted text.

1\. Identify the applicable locations from the dropdown list \*(Location-wise

basis)\* and indicate it in a separate Column for pricers reference

2\. Tag this column as "\*Remark (Customer0\_)\*"

Pricers should consider and select all three port of discharge options and

provide their offer for the respective port pair. If we consolidate the

dropdown values into a separate column and map them in Eagle X, pricers

might select a "Port of Discharge" that does not apply to the respective

cell. This could create an additional task for the In-Tender and Trade

teams to verify the actual cell value. We are working under a very tight

deadline for this tender, which needs to be uploaded to the customer

portal. Therefore, it is crucial that each cell value is accurate to avoid

last-minute follow-ups.

\[image: image.png\]

different cell to cell drop down values.

including but not limited to the European Union (EU), United States of

America, and IMO, on reducing greenhouse gas emissions by adding container

shipping to the Emissions Trading System (ETS), there may be an increase

expected in the overall shipping cost. Subject to the latest developments,

ONE may implement a surcharge or revise the base freight in accordance with

the additional cost of such compliance. ONE will ensure cost transparency

towards our customers in case such regulation comes into effect. If you

have any questions, please do not hesitate to contact our Sales

Representatives.

Hi Giselle,

trust you are well,

with FrieslandCampina we had a similar issue concerning following;

In case customers use platforms for their tender bids such as

FrieslandCampina and STOLT using KEELVAR

it is not always clear what input is exactly requested, hence pricers go in

with best of their knowledge and what seems logical.

Overall pricers should stick to details in Customer requests (T\&C) and ONE

AGREED Instructions as pe rbelow

\[image: image.png\]

Once consolidated file is received , GAM/CKAM does the upload in the

platform and any discrepancies have to be filtered, checked and correctly

input.

This can go from words having to start with a capital letter (or not),

correct shortcodes, only accepting numbers iso words (or other way around..

etc, etc

In both cases with Friesland Campina and STOLT it seems that the 1st Round

feedback sheet (with all the corrected details mentioned and columns added

with Feedback rates) is offered via Eagle X Check in form and re-worked by

Eagle X team.

However in both cases FC and STOLT tenders were received back after pricers

input for Round 2 and "old" incomplete details had overwritten the input

that GAM/CKAM corrected from the first offer, which then results in

discrepancies again which have to be corrected as otherwise upload can not

be done.

In both cases, Bart and I were able to copy the correct details back into

the R2 offer again but this of course is not idle especially when pricers

are not committing to deadlines.

Kindly asking you to check if this situation has occurred before.

## CLV Impact: \~10bps Drop in KPI-SLA Adherence

受信: Tue Feb 11 2025 11:51:08 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daniel Woo \<daniel.woo@one-line.com\>  
Hi Masuda-san,

As of yesterday, the dashboard for CLV Performance Monitoring has been

done, which is located in the \*"FY25 Eagle X Dashboard \- Failure Analysis

(Conversion)"\* storypoint. Nakai-san has shown attention on

CLV's performance lately, so I believe it is a matter of time till he

directs us to improve CLV performance (which will directly improve

Conversion Cycle Time & Quality). Rather than doing this reactively, we

need to take proactive actions. Basically as of now, three potential issues

with CLV (I have informed Sang about these, and he will work with William

on addressing these issues):

\*1) Data Inaccuracy Issue for Receiving Time and Resolving Time\*

\- About 15% of issues are resolved within 10 minutes, which is a huge

concern.

\- CLV reports a 3-hour average resolution time, but this is skewed by

easier cases. For LIVE Conversion, the actual average is 5.4 hours.

\- Additionally, CLV Receiving Time is logged when issues enter the

Enquiries sheet, not when users raise them.

\- Accounting for these factors, the \*real cycle time for LIVE Conversion

issues is 6–8 hours\*, which is unacceptable.

\[image: image.png\]

\[image: image.png\]

\*2) Most Conversion Tool Errors have no Future Development Plans\*

\- Three out of four errors lack permanent solutions.

\- CLV remains reactive, addressing issues only when users report problems

or when directed by the Eagle-X team. Without proactive problem-solving,

CLV limits Eagle-X's ability to scale.

\[image: image.png\]

\*3) A Large Majority of Conversion Tool Errors have No Classifications\*

\- This further reinforces the idea that CLV is not proactively resolving

the cases (because if they do, they would have classified the issues

accordingly).

\- Following the DMAIC process, if CLV does not even begin by defining the

problem, it is highly likely that no improvement plans will be initiated by

them, and the same error will only occur repeatedly.

\[image: image.png\]

If all three issues can be resolved from the CLV side, the \*average KPI-SLA

adherence rate should go \>70%\* as a result of higher efficiency and lower

number of errors in the future. This information will be beneficial to

Nakai-san as well but it is better for you to determine if it is

appropriate to share this information at this point.

\-- 

Thanks & Regards,

Daniel Woo

\--

## Re: CLV Impact: \~10bps Drop in KPI-SLA Adherence

受信: Wed Feb 12 2025 15:31:58 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daniel Woo \<daniel.woo@one-line.com\>  
Hi Masuda-san,

Here are some new discoveries, particularly about Receiving Time inaccuracy

(more info to be found HERE

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1It8vEArbchcwRj8t7184NzyMphBVuRQ6mOYcRzzpxsY/edit?gid=0\#gid=0\>

):

\[image: image.png\]

All checked cases \*mismatch \*the actual Receiving Time.

\- Delays likely stem from CLV inactivity around midnight, causing late

entries in the User Inquiries sheet.

\- Early cases likely result from Vietnam-Singapore time zone differences,

with the script capturing Vietnam time (1 hour ahead).

Regardless, the mismatch issue has to be resolved. I will inform Sang on

this matter.

Also, here are three issues I have collected from CLV side, which will help

managements understand CLV low performance better:

\*1) Lack of a Business Analyst to Facilitate communication between Users

and Developers\*

\- There is no clear communication channel between Eagle-X users and

developers, causing misunderstandings in terms of requirements.

\- Change management aspect of development is weak, leading to unnecessary

halted or delayed developments due to constant shifting of requirements.

\- User requests are not properly translated into technical specifications,

resulting in unnecessary rework of developers.

\*2) Non-Compliance of Escalation Procedures of Users\*

\- To resolve issues quickly, users must CC the team lead (William) to

ensure they are properly logged.

\- However, some users forget to do this despite multiple reminders, causing

issues to be overlooked.

\*3) Communication Gaps in DevOps between Tereda-san Team and CLV\*

\- Important enhancement request details were not shared with CLV before

testing, causing delays.

\- Tereda-san’s team made changes without informing CLV, leading to

unexpected issues and longer troubleshooting.

\- The latest enhancement request versions were not provided, causing a

mismatch between development and actual requirements.

\---------- Forwarded message \---------

From: Kasia Stannard \<kasia.stannard@one-line.com\>

Date: Mon, 10 Feb 2025 at 16:39

Subject: Re: Eagle X target candidates for March '25

To: Andy Brice \<andy.brice@one-line.com\>

Cc: EUA.SYM.YM \<eua.sym.ym@one-line.com\>, Jay Hardiman \<

jay.hardiman@one-line.com\>, EUA EAGLEX \<eua.eaglex@one-line.com\>

Hi Andy,

Cannot say I disagree with you from the process standardisation &

efficiency point of view.

However there are some mitigating circumstances \- it's not so much about NA

Sales/Pricers who do not want to handle tenders via EX but more about

concerns about OMMC/WNS IN who handle mostly GKA/Hyper-care accounts. With

Jan-March being peak season globally & GKA BCO handled by them being huge

tenders involving many trades, there have been some issues with the quality

of the consolidated data produced by thos teams. New product details being

fixed so late does not help as well (we have many instances of Pricer

indicating old product, tenders teams not being obliged to verify/rectify

those & then C-KAMs scrambling last minute to update new product details).

After receiving a few consolidated files with many errors, NA MNGT

requested to have some exception for GKA A/Cs while leaving on-shore bids

via Eagle X \- & right now with volumes of bids GHQ EX was not able to

guarantee OMMC/WNS IN immediate improvement so they reluctantly agreed. Out

of the total 314 NA Controlled A/Cs, 210 are on-shore handled via CST so

will remain via EX while some of 104 GKA accounts will now convert to AS-IS

process (some were already handled via EX in Dec-Feb).

GHQ EX team is trying to support WNS IN/OMMC as much as possible to improve

consolidated data quality but the tender peak along with the new product is

proving too much right now.

FYR \- we had similar issues with the BASF consolidated file on Fri &

OMMC/GHQ EX were assisting us with correcting the file \- finally uploading

it at 19.30 UK time\!

For EUA we have 2 GKA A/Cs for March \- Mars & Mercedes: Mars was confirmed

today to handle AS-IS while Mercedes will be reviewed.

I will share your concerns with the GHQ EX team so they are aware that NA

exception will have a downstream impact on the workload of Pricing teams

around the globe.

Thank you.

Best regards,

## Re: Eagle X target candidates for March '25

受信: Thu Feb 20 2025 18:36:45 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kazuki Masuda \<kazuki.masuda@one-line.com\>  
Dear all,

Thank you for your continued support of Eagle X.

We have received inquiries from several users, so let us share the current

scope of the NA accounts.

For NA \*Offshore\* Accounts, it has been agreed at the management level that

these will continue to be conducted under ASIS, rather than Eagle X.

However, NA \*Onshore\* Accounts will continue to be conducted under Eagle X

as before.

We apologize for any confusion regarding these categories.

Simply if an account is not grayed out on the target list, it remains

within the scope.

This list is continuously updated, so please refer to it if you have any

questions.

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qzMdUlX59ZWbwi9sFTqGO\_B2QBs7PZxQCLmR2E9VDXw/edit?gid=107478763\#gid=107478763

Kazuki Masuda

\*LA Inland Remarks (In case LA Inland involved):\*

\*Does not include cost of 3 axles chassis or other additional costs.

\*All inland rates are subject to all applicable surcharges as per LA

\*All rates are subject to transport and equipment availability.

\*Special cargo (OOG, OOW, 45' FOOT, Isotanks, IMO, multi stops, additional

logistics, drop and pick, bobtail, etc) must be quoted on a case by case.

\*It's important to note that we expect a possible increase of 10-20% for

the client’s requested long-term cases due to factors such as rising diesel

costs, local currency depreciation, increases on specific routes based on

market conditions, etc. We recommend always adding a margin to the inland

freight costs for long-term scenarios to account for any potential

increases during the period, as there is a strong tendency for costs across

all vendors to rise. However, MKTG has the flexibility to determine the

best approach and pricing strategy to secure these volumes and maintain the

account.

Hi Elton and Ada,

Thank you for your time today.

We referred to TP Domi-JP R2 Pricing Tool working file and managed to

retrieve the mentioned offer under ONE Lane ID \= NEW\_TP\_Domi-CIF-JP\_001. We

have also verified that it was correctly exported and submitted as R2

Pricer Submission file (please disregard blank information in columns AT-BX

as the corresponding lanes are not present in R2 customer tender file).

\[image: image.png\]

Unfortunately, the consolidation tool failed to capture ONE Lane ID \=

NEW\_TP\_Domi-CIF-JP\_001, along with other new lanes / alternative POD

offers, due to limitations in logic between Pricer Submission file and

Consolidation Tool. We are analysing the problem and implementing

corrective measures to ensure we capture all offered lanes, including new

lanes, and prevent future occurrences.

\[image: image.png\]

On the other hand, regarding JP tenders, JP Sales is responsible for

transferring Pricer Offers from the consolidated file into the original

customer tender upon receipt. We are seeking to understand why the

discrepancy between the consolidated file and the customer sheet was not

detected by Sales and will follow up separately.

Please accept our apologies for the misinput, which has placed TP MKTG in a

challenging situation. We have initiated a review of our internal

procedures to ensure this does not recur.

as the corresponding lanes are not present in R2 customer tender file).

\[image: image.png\]

Unfortunately, the consolidation tool failed to capture ONE Lane ID \=

NEW\_TP\_Domi-CIF-JP\_001, along with other new lanes / alternative POD

offers, due to limitations in logic between Pricer Submission file and

Consolidation Tool. We are analysing the problem and implementing

corrective measures to ensure we capture all offered lanes, including new

lanes, and prevent future occurrences.

\[image: image.png\]

On the other hand, regarding JP tenders, JP Sales is responsible for

transferring Pricer Offers from the consolidated file into the original

customer tender upon receipt. We are seeking to understand why the

discrepancy between the consolidated file and the customer sheet was not

detected by Sales and will follow up separately.

Please accept our apologies for the misinput, which has placed TP MKTG in a

challenging situation. We have initiated a review of our internal

procedures to ensure this does not recur.

\<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/eaglex/pricer-resources\>

Best Regards,

\*Flourance Tan\*

Strategic Yield Management

Eagle X Project

## Re: \[Eagle X-LIVE-FY25\] Final Consolidated Offer \_ G-JP100734 \_ DENSO \_ seq01 \_ R2

受信: Thu Feb 06 2025 20:47:53 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kazuki Masuda \<kazuki.masuda@one-line.com\>  
Dear Elton and Fukai san,

We apologize for any inconvenience caused by this case.

The situation involves multiple complex factors, making it difficult to

fully explain via email.

Please find below a summary of the causes. If you require additional

details, I will explain it separately in a meeting.

(1) \*Misalignment between CKAM and CST regarding changes to the R2 customer

file\*

   \- Initially, the R1 Additional Lanes were included in the original

   submitted customer file. However, after CKAM communicated with CST, CKAM

   removed the Additional Lanes which include the lines POD \= LAX. As a

   result, once consolidation took place, there was no corresponding row to

   return the pricing results for the new lane. Consequently, the current

   Consolidation tool could not automatically feed back the newly added lane’s

   pricing results.

   \- (Our assumption) Instead, CKAM manually changed the original lane’s

   POD from Tacoma to LAX. CST did not notice this change and assigned the

   same Lane ID from R1 during the R2 conversion. As a result, the Pricing

   tool continued to treat this lane as Tacoma and was unable to process LAX

   as a new lane.

\*(Next Action) \* We do not want CKAM to delete existing lanes. If anything

   needs to be added, we would like CKAM to add it as a new lane below.

   We will update our SOP that CST must include the POD as part of the key

   when assigning Lane IDs, and we will ensure them to follow it.

   \-

   (Original submitted R2 customer file)

   \[image: image.png\]

    The original customer file for POD contained two lanes: Tacoma and

   LAX.

   (Updated R2 customer file)

   \[image: image.png\]

   In the updated customer file, the LAX lane was deleted, and the lane

   that was originally Tacoma was updated to LAX. (Assumption)

(2) \*Inability to detect the issue during Consolidation\*

   \- Although the Pricing tool still had the R1 Additional Lane, since

   there was no corresponding row after removal, it was not output to the

   Consolidation file, making the issue undetectable. Under other region's

   operation, CST would copy and paste the data afterward, providing an

   opportunity to notice the added lane. However, due to a Japan-specific

   operation where CKAM handles the copy-and-paste, this went unnoticed.

   \*(Next Action)\*

   When there is an Additional Lane in the Pricing tool, we will change the

   process so that CST explicitly highlights any added lanes to CKAM. (We will

   also enhance the tool to make such additions more readily identifiable.)

In summary, this issue arose due to a combination of unexpected file

updates by CKAM, errors on CST’s conversion, and a unique operational

method in Japan.

We sincerely regret any inconvenience this has caused and appreciate your

understanding.

If you have any further questions or concerns, please let us know.

Thanks & Regards,

Kazuki Masuda

(--- 引用省略 \---)  
---

growing both globally and regionally. In order to comply with the latest

but not limited to the European Union (EU), United States of America, and

IMO, on reducing greenhouse gas emissions by adding container shipping to

the overall shipping cost. Subject to the latest developments, ONE may

towards our customers in case such regulation comes into effect. If you

## Re: (Round 2\) A/C Honda Motor \- 2025/2026 Tender Preparation Action Items & Deadline

受信: Tue Jan 14 2025 13:16:05 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kazuki Masuda \<kazuki.masuda@one-line.com\>  
Dear Iio san and Sakuma san,

We apologize for the delayed response and for the challenges with the R2

process in Eagle X, which resulted in lost time.

Below is our root cause analysis and proposed action plan moving forward.

Background & Issue

   1\.

   \*Linking R1 and R2 (Lane ID)\*

   Eagle X requires linking R1 and R2, specifically identifying which Lane

   is new and which is deleted (Lane ID). Under normal circumstances, Eagle X

   provides a supplemental tool called the “R2 Supplemental Tool” to

   streamline the identification of Lane IDs. If used properly, it allows the

   Lane IDs to be organized quickly and without significant effort.

   2\.

   \*Issue in the HONDA Case\*

   In the HONDA case, there was a deviation from the usual workflow. After

   the R1 conversion was completed, an error in the OMMC conversion

   (specifically in the Field Mapping for POR) was discovered. During the fix,

   the updating other related mappings was overlooked (i.e., after correcting

   the Field Mapping, the Place Mapping also needed to be updated). This

   oversight caused the Lane IDs in R1 to become completely disordered—an

   issue we did not recognize until the R2 phase began.

   3\.

   \*Impact on R2 Conversion\*

   When conducting the R2 conversion, the R1 Lane IDs were already in

   disarray, making it impossible to use the R2 Supplemental Tool. Although

   the Eagle X team attempted to manually reconcile the Lane IDs, the process

   required a full manual re-organization of R1’s Lane IDs, resulting in

   significantly more time than usual. Given the pricing deadlines, Eagle X

   team decided to switch to the AS-IS approach.

Action Items

   1\.

   \*Reinforce Eagle X Reviews\*

   Enhance the Eagle X review process to ensure potential Field Mapping

   issues are identified and addressed promptly.

   2\.

   \*Retraining for OMMC Team on R2 Processes\*

   Provide refresher training to the OMMC team on the R2 workflow and

   proper usage of the R2 Supplemental Tool.

   3\.

   \*Training on Conversion Tool Modifications for OMMC\*

   Train the OMMC team on identifying and updating interrelated components

   when modifying the Conversion Tool, ensuring no steps are missed.

If you have any questions, let me know anytime.

Thanks & Regards,

Kazuki Masuda

(--- 引用省略 \---)  
---

Issues which we had this year

R1 : We lost much time in the OMMC conversion and consolidation . The

Pricing team had little time to submit 1st offer in Eagle X and We(Sales

team) could not receive offers from them by deadline and we had no time to

review 1st offer rate level.

R2 : We lost much time in the OMMC conversion and as the result of changing

to the  AS-IS format, Pricing team quoted manually from R2 and the wrong

rate structure issues occured in various trades and we could not recognize

its error until Final Round.

Final : We found the wrong rate structure issues and  we had to increase

offer rates from R2. We have never asked Honda to raise the offer rates. We

were told by customers that with so many rate errors, they could not trust

ONE's offer.

I have heard that one of the causes was changes of Lane ID No. / Origin or

Destination between R1 and R2 by Honda.

Unfortunately, I checked with Honda and they say there is a possibility to

change Lane ID No. / Origin / Destination even next year and beyond.

We will have to follow the same timeline as this year from next year (There

is no time to lose.)

problem will occur next year. What are your thoughts on this?

Unless EagleX's specifications change, I think that Honda's bid should be

removed from EagleX format from next year onwards.

further ensure both speed and quality.

## Fwd: (Round 2\) A/C Honda Motor \- 2025/2026 Tender Preparation Action Items & Deadline

受信: Fri Mar 14 2025 09:54:56 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daisuke Tsunematsu \<daisuke.tsunematsu@one-line.com\>  
関係者各位、

念の為補足します。今期のホンダのExecutionの総括として、たしかにOMMCの習熟度の改善は必須ですが、

” there was a lack of

proficiency”だけでは問題の本質を正確に補足しきれておらず、また必ずしもトレーニングだけで乗り越えられる問題でないとも考えています。

当方で認識している事実関係は以下の通り。OMMCとしても来期の実践に向けてレヴューと対策を打って行きたいと考えています。

\*R1\*

● リリース前に当時GCSMからフォーマットのCompexityに関する懸念について指摘が入るも、GHQ及びJP SYMの合意の下、Eagle

X決行を決定。

● OMMCがコンバージョンに費やした日数は4日。 Complexity を踏まえるとガイドラインは4日で（Standard 2 days \+ 1

day for more than 10 pricer involved \+ 1 day for more than 1,000

lanes)、OMMCとしては一応はガイドラインにフォローできた形だったが、ホンダR1のReleaseは11/1、Deadlineは11/18であり持ち時間は12WD、後工程の時間確保を考えるとさらに迅速なリリースが必要だった。

● Conversion後のONE Format上のColumn数は、例えばAEWでは600行を超え、Pricer Input

Columnは100行を超える事態となった

● PricerはホンダのRate Structureを勘案できず、Pricer Offerのデータが超絶的に混乱。（Pricer

Behaviorの問題はホンダに限らず抜本的な対処が必要だが、しかしながら600以上のコラムをチェックして100行以上のPricer

Input Columnに対応せよというのはいずれにせよ現実的でない）

● CKAMが休日返上、寝る間も惜しんで修正作業を強いられる事態となった。

改善提案

（プロセス及びツールの改善）

● Pricer OfferのQualityの問題 ＞ Pricing Tool上にValidation機能を設置

● コンバージョン後のColumn数が多すぎる ＞ 特にホンダの様なケースにおいて、コラム数をどう集約できるか考える必要あり

● Pre Conversion Study ＞ Conversionの可否のみならず、特に今期トラブルのあったテンダーについては、Data

QualityやプロセスのFeasibilityも点検する必要あり

（トレーニング）

● Pricing ToolのManipulationやInterpretationの問題 ＞ 習熟度の問題、トレーニングの実施

● コンバージョンタイムの改善 ＞ TSTの習熟度の問題。トレーニングの実施

\*R2\*

● R1のデータをR2データにマッピングできず、R2リリース後にAS ISへの方針転換があった

改善提案

● R1からR2へのデータの受け渡しの標準化、簡素化

Best regards,

□-------------------------------------------------------------------□

\*Daisuke Tsunematsu  /  常松 大輔\*

Global Tender Management (GTM)

OMMC

Mobile \+63 9188074023

## Re: (Round 2\) A/C Honda Motor \- 2025/2026 Tender Preparation Action Items & Deadline

受信: Fri Mar 14 2025 17:37:04 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Sumiyo Iio \<sumiyo.iio@one-line.com\>  
常松さん

（CC：増田さん、皆様）

お忙しい中、今回の経緯と問題点の整理を頂きまして、ありがとうございます。

以下のご理解で異論ございません。

ホンダのBID sheetはレーン数も多く、またRate Structureも複雑です。

また申し上げた通り、来年度以降も、Roundと途中でReference ID Noが変わってしまったり、

仕向け地が変わることも起こりうるので、おっしゃる通り、OMMCへのトレーニングだけではカバーできないこともあると思っています。

一方で一部でも来期に向けた、システム改修も期待できるのではと思い、その辺りの進捗状況も踏まえて

8月頃に改めてお伺いさせて頂きたい次第です。（システム自体の改善状況とOMMCの習熟度アップの状況）

また今回明らかになったのはPricing teamの質とレスポンスの悪さです。彼らの習熟度も大きな問題です。

加えてR1のみEagle Xを通し、R2からAS ISに変更することこそ、Pricerにとっては負担かつ、サーチャージ構成の誤りが多発しますので、

来期以降は、全RoundをEagle Xを通すか通さないかを最初に決めるべきだと強く思います。

ホンダは2025年度、大きくシェアを伸ばせた一方で来年以降はこのシェアを死守していかなければならず、

来年度以降も今回のような状況の中、運賃交渉をしなければならないとすると非常にしんどいと思いますので、

その辺りも含めてご相談させてください。

引き続き、何卒宜しくお願い致します。

\[image: 埋め込み画像 2\]
